< text>
This is a great pool option for you. They keep the pool very warm which is great for arthritis. If you have a disability you can use these pools easily as they are specially designed for you to be able to access the pool. They have water aerobics and physical therapy and it's really a nice crowd that goes there. The administrative staff is very nice and helpful. It's $325 per year but you can go all you want</text>

<name>Pretty Kitti<//name><resp>None< /resp><Rating>4< /Rating>< pics>
None<//pics>
<Text>Love the warm water! It's really nice that the supply so many different kinds of safety vest, supports, noodles, weights, paddle boards just anything to keep you comfortable, safe & relaxed while your in the water.

The life guards are nice as well as the water therapist. The staff are very positive, encouraging and focus to help you no matter what your going through!

Pools of Hope isn't just for people with disabilities, it's for everyone! The young, old, doesn't matter what your skin tone is.

They also have to pools, a lap pool and a large general pool! They have lifts for both oools. They only thing I feel it needs is a larger ladies dressing room and another shower. They currently have two.

Over all it's a great pool and staff!</Text></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
I am surviving Multiple Sclerosis, and although many people with MS are heat sensitive, as am I, the warm waters are doing wonders for me.  My Therapist has given me exercises, that awaken muscles that I haven't felt work in years. I believe that with the warm water and the therapy, my mobility is improving.  I thank God for the California Aquatic Therapy Center/California Pools of Hope.<//Review>

< rate>
5<//rate>
< Review>
So our second stop was at the Julian Pioneer Museum. This place is run by volunteers and there is a $3 donation fee, not bad at all. There is no actual parking in this property but there is street parking, if you are lucky enough to find any that is lol.
This is quite a small place but it is filled with a lot of old information from this town. From the original pioneers, many old artifacts, how they cooked, the kind of clothes they wore. What was surprising is that they actually have a lot of things that are not closed up in display cases. Mostly everything here has a sign for you not to touch anything, which is understandable all this stuff is really old. There is a table in the front that they will let you touch though lol it's of dead animals fur and snake skin lol.
It's was very informative and interesting for a very small place< /Review>

< Review>
A spectacular shop full of talented artists and piercers!

Ben did a wonderful job on a small, hand-written word on my right wrist/forearm, and I can't say enough about Perry's warmth and professionalism. He helped me rehab a *terrible* daith (that piercer had lied to me about their level of experience and the quality of their jewelry, but that's another story), and he was eventually able to re-pierce it properly with a gorgeous gold ring. He also did my nostril piercing, and both are now healing beautifully. Mel at the counter is absolutely delightful and will always make an effort to see you promptly even during the shop's (often) hectic days.

Rose Gold's is my go-to shop in SF, and I can't recommend them highly enough!

<date>1517324917235<//date><rate>5<//rate><Review>After having poured through different photos for a few weeks, I came in here with a few ideas of piercings I wanted, but was uncertain which were actually possible with the shape of my ear. Perry was able to quickly take a look at my ear and rule some out, and suggest others which could work better for me.

I decided to go with a forward helix piercing, but when it came time to pick jewelry, I fell in love with an oval piece that wouldn't work for the piercing I had in mind. Perry took a look at it and said "this would be perfect in a conch piercing" and held it up for me to see. I loved the way it looked, but I hadn't gotten a piercing in 10 years and was worried about the pain and healing (conches seem painful to me, idk why). He assured me it was an easy piercing and healing process so I decided to do it. He was absolutely right. He did the piercing in a split second, and it was the least painful piercing I've ever had. The first thing I said was "woah you're really good!" and the second was "I've had flu shots more painful than that". 10/10 would recommend coming here for a piercing.

The thing I love most is the placement. The jewelry faces forward and is always visible, but looks great from the side too. It catches the light and really adds some character. Can't wait to come back and get some piercings on the other ear!

A note on pricing: all of the jewelry they sell is fine metals, diamonds, and semi precious stones. For the simplest plain ball, you're looking at 60ish dollars, but for anything else, it seemed like the pricepoint was between $100-200 and much more for the really bling-y pieces (there was one in there I adored that was $550). They have simple diamond studs, but they don't pierce with the smallest size, so you need to buy at least the medium size, which was ~$130 (the large was $150 I think). I'm in the phase of my life were I want nice things that'll last, so I thought it was worth it, but definitely be willing to shell out if you come here to be pierced.</Review><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPhhrRlI38I8_4wTZHJikZek4-TLa2_B34iS9PV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures>< response>

<Review>We discovered the design your own pizza. Yum. Only missing ingredient is pineapple. LOL. Yes, Im one of THOSE people, I enjoy pineapple on my pizza!

We used to get the hot and ready - only cheese and pepperoni. For only a few dollars more you can design your own.
So worth it!! You must use the app on your cell to get this. Also, if you use the app, you can order a 2-liter soda, and with a code, there will be no charge for your soda. Bonus!

Only issue is, (and why I deducted two stars) the pizza is never the same two times on a row. One time its cooked to perfection,  but short on the toppings, next time, it's undercooked, or burned on the bottom, or even lukewarm when picked up. Once on a blue moon everything comes together and you get a delicious cooked pizza, including the toppings, steaming hot, with lots of toppings on a perfectly baked crust.  Yum!

If you havent tried Little Caesars Pizza, I suggest you give them a try! You might be surprised how much money you save.<//Review>< response>
